When you stop the function clicking on \"Stop follow me\", the route will not be stored in the device. This way, if you go from point B to point A, you can follow a route on map previously stored and loaded (follow back).\r\n\r\n4) Replay route on the map (a route previously stored in step 2). In this way, when you are at home, you can replay a travel. Seeing the params as (course, speed, altitude). \r\n\r\nIf you are a tourist, this app will be useful to the holidays and leisure time.
